idle = {
	male = {
		default = { head = "idle_entry" torso = "idle_entry" }
		
		# Warcraft
		still = {
			animation = { head = "still" torso = "still" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = 2000
					has_no_animations_trigger = yes
				}
			}
		}

		# Warcraft
		AI_hunchbacked = {
			animation = { head = "idle_entry" torso = "idle_entry" }

			weight = {
				base = 0

				modifier = {
					add = 110
		 			portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = hunchbacked }
				}
			}
		}

		AI_idle_infant = {
			animation = { head = "idle_entry" torso = "idleInfant_entry" }

			weight = {
				base = 0

				modifier = {
					add = 100
					# Warcraft
					scope:age <= age_5_value
				}
			}
		}

		AI_idle_child = {
			animation = { head = "idle_entry" torso = "idleInfant_entry" }

			weight = {
				base = 0

				modifier = {
					add = 100
					always = no #scope:age <= age_9_value

				}
			}
		}

		AI_idle_basic = {
			animation = { head = "idle_entry" torso = "idle_entry" }

			weight = {
				base = 0

				modifier = {
					add = 99
					# Warcraft
					#scope:age >= age_10_value
					scope:current_weight <= 75
				}
			}
		}

		AI_idle_fat = {
			animation = { head = "idle_entry" torso = "idleFat_entry" }

				base = 0

				modifier = {
					add = 100
					# Warcraft
					#scope:age >= age_10_value
					scope:current_weight >= 75
				}
			}
		}

		AI_honorable = {
			animation = { head = "AI_honorable_entry" torso = "AI_honorable_entry" }

			weight = {
				base = 0

				# Score set to 100 + the actual ai_value score (will range from 150 to 200)
				modifier = {
					add = {
						value = 100
						add = scope:ai_honor
					}
					# Warcraft
					#scope:age >= age_10_value
					scope:ai_honor >= max_positive_honor
					scope:current_weight <= 50
					NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = dwarf } }
					NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant } }
					portrait_wear_armor_trigger = no
					portrait_mena_clothing_trigger = no

		AI_dishonorable = {
			animation = { head = "AI_dishonorable_entry" torso = "AI_dishonorable_entry" }

			weight = {
				base = 0

				# Score set to 100 + the inverse of the negative ai_value score (will range from 150 to 200)
				modifier = {
					add = {
						value = 100
						add = {
							value = ai_honor
							multiply = -1
						}
					}
					# Warcraft
					#scope:age >= age_10_value
					scope:ai_honor <= max_negative_honor
					scope:current_weight <= 20
					NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = dwarf } }
					NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant } }
					portrait_wear_armor_trigger = no
					portrait_mena_clothing_trigger = no                
				}
			}

			portrait_modifier = {							# Triggered portrait modifier for when this animation is picked. The first one satisfying the trigger will be picked.
				animations = AI_dishonorable_decal				# One or multiple portrait modifier overrides
			}
		}

# misc_pregnantSerious_entry (above) is for characeters with negative traits
#
# misc_pregnant_entry (below) is for characters with positive traits
#
# we had to put pregnant triggers all the way down here because we need to prioritize playing misc_pregnantSerious_entry. hence, you can find misc_pregnantSerious_entry above.
# 

 		AI_pregnant_dwarf_or_armor = {
			animation = { head = "misc_pregnant_entry" torso = "misc_pregnantFat_entry" }

			weight = {
				base = 0

				modifier = {
					add = 100
					OR = {
						portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = dwarf }
						portrait_wear_armor_trigger = yes
					}
					portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant }
				}
			}
		}

		AI_pregnant = {
			animation = { head = "misc_pregnant_entry" torso = "misc_pregnant_entry" }

			weight = {
				base = 0

				modifier = {
					add = 100
					portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant }
					NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = dwarf } }
				}
			}
		}
    }

	boy = male
	female = male
	girl = male
}

aggressive_axe = { # wields one handed axe
	male = {
		default = { head = "emotion_oneHandedAggressive1_entry" torso = "emotion_oneHandedAggressive1_entry" }
		
		# Warcraft
		still = {
			animation = { head = "still" torso = "still" }
			weight = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = 2000
					has_no_animations_trigger = yes
				}
			}
		}
		
		emotion_one_handed_aggressive_axe_infant = {
			animation = { head = "idle" torso = "idleInfant_entry" }

			weight = {
				base = 0

				modifier = {
					add = 100
					scope:age <= age_5_value
				}
			}
		}

		emotion_one_handed_aggressive_axe_child = {
			animation = { head = "idle_entry" torso = "idle_entry" }

			weight = {
				base = 0

				modifier = {
					add = 100
					always = no #scope:age <= age_9_value

				}
			}
		}

		emotion_one_handed_aggressive_axe_basic = {
			animation = { head = "emotion_oneHandedAggressive1_entry" torso = "emotion_oneHandedAggressive1_entry" }

			weight = {
				base = 0

				modifier = {
					add = 100
					AND = {
						scope:current_weight < 50
						NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = dwarf } }
						NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant } }
                        
					}
				}
			}

			portrait_modifier = {
				trigger = {
					any_equipped_character_artifact = { artifact_type = axe }
				}
				animations = AI_vengeful_decal
				animations_props = artifact_axe_equipped_prop
			}

			portrait_modifier = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = { any_equipped_character_artifact = { artifact_type = axe } }
					culture = { has_clothing_gfx = northern_clothing_gfx }
				}			
				animations_props = artisan_axe_northern_pagan_prop
				animations = AI_vengeful_decal
			}
			
			portrait_modifier = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = { any_equipped_character_artifact = { artifact_type = axe } }
					culture = {	has_clothing_gfx = indian_clothing_gfx }
				}			
				animations_props = artisan_axe_indian_prop
				animations = AI_vengeful_decal
			}
			
			portrait_modifier = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = { any_equipped_character_artifact = { artifact_type = axe } }
					culture = {
						OR = {
							has_clothing_gfx = african_clothing_gfx
							has_clothing_gfx = mena_clothing_gfx
							has_clothing_gfx = mongol_clothing_gfx
						}
					}
				}			
				animations_props = artisan_axe_mena_prop
				animations = AI_vengeful_decal
			}
			
			portrait_modifier = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = { any_equipped_character_artifact = { artifact_type = axe } }
					axe_unique_gfx_trigger = no
				}			
				animations_props = artisan_axe_prop
				animations = AI_vengeful_decal
			}
		}	

		emotion_one_handed_aggressive_axe_fat = {
			animation = { head = "emotion_oneHandedAggressive1_entry" torso = "emotion_oneHandedAggressive1_entry" }

			weight = {
				base = 0

				modifier = {
					add = 100
					AND = {
						scope:current_weight > 50
						NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = dwarf } }
						NOT = { portrait_has_trait_trigger = { TRAIT = pregnant } }
                        
					}					
				}
			}

			portrait_modifier = {
				trigger = {
					any_equipped_character_artifact = { artifact_type = axe }
				}
				animations = AI_vengeful_decal
				animations_props = artifact_axe_equipped_prop
			}

			portrait_modifier = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = { any_equipped_character_artifact = { artifact_type = axe } }
					culture = { has_clothing_gfx = northern_clothing_gfx }
				}			
				animations_props = artisan_axe_northern_pagan_prop
				animations = AI_vengeful_decal
			}
			
			portrait_modifier = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = { any_equipped_character_artifact = { artifact_type = axe } }
					culture = {	has_clothing_gfx = indian_clothing_gfx }
				}			
				animations_props = artisan_axe_indian_prop
				animations = AI_vengeful_decal
			}
			
			portrait_modifier = {
				trigger = {
					NOT = { any_equipped_character_artifact = { artifact_type = axe } }
					culture = {
						OR = {
							has_clothing_gfx = african_clothing_gfx
							has_clothing_gfx = mena_clothing_gfx
							has_clothing_gfx = mongol_clothing_gfx
						}

				}			
				animations_props = artisan_spear_prop_right_hand

			}
		}
	}
